```text
# Verdict
NEEDS_FIX

The change under review is `368262d → a5ed4ff` ("Add E2E generated-target glossary routing"): it fills in the previously no-op `_after_translation_tick` to write generated target text into `router_text_window`/`router_text_source`, drops the `common_terms` base slice (`base_slice: none`, `type: diagnostic`), simplifies `_autoterm_base_preset`, and adds Chinese topic keywords for nlp/medicine only. The base-slice removal and the external-source guard are correct and tested. But the generated-target routing path has a real functional gap for two of the four advertised domains, a precision/self-reinforcement risk that is untested, and its central correctness claim ("one routing tick behind") cannot be confirmed from the packet.

# Must fix before merge

### 1. Generated-target routing cannot switch to finance/legal for a Chinese target (silent dead path)
- **Severity:** High (spec mismatch / hidden functional gap)
- **Where:** `framework/agents/term_memory/domain_taxonomy.py` `DOMAIN_TOPIC_KEYWORDS`; consumed by `topic_keyword_scores` → `HybridWindowTopicRouter._score_hybrid`.
- **Why real:** The default `auto_glossary_presets` is `nlp_core_10k,medicine_core_10k,finance_core_10k,legal_core_10k`, and the new production signal is the *generated target* window, which for the default `English -> Chinese` pair is Chinese. This commit adds Chinese keywords to the `nlp` and `medicine` blocks only. The `finance` and `legal` blocks remain English-only (`\bmarket(s)?\b`, `\bcourt(s)?\b`, …). Python `\b`-anchored English regex never matches Chinese text, so `text_topic_score` for finance/legal is identically 0 on any Chinese generated target. The router therefore can never route *to* finance or legal via the generated-target path — the exact "deployable E2E route" this change is built to provide. The docs and paper wording claim the router "switches the active domain slice" among the domain inventory without stating that two of the four domains are unreachable through the shipping signal.
- **How to verify:** Feed a Chinese finance/legal generated-target window (e.g. 市场/股票/利率 or 法院/合同/管辖权) through `HybridWindowTopicRouter.observe(..., router_text_source="generated_target")` from a `finance`/`legal` starting state; confirm `text_topic_score` and any switch. There is no such test in `test_hybrid_window_topic_router.py` (only the nlp→medicine Chinese case).
- **Minimal fix direction:** Add Chinese finance/legal topic keywords symmetric with nlp/medicine, or explicitly scope the E2E generated-target claim/docs to the domains that actually have target-language coverage.

### 2. "One routing tick behind" guarantee is unverifiable and is the correctness hinge of the feature
- **Severity:** High if the call ordering is wrong (self-reinforcement becomes immediate)
- **Where:** `framework/agents/omni.py` `_after_translation_tick` (writes `router_text_window`) vs `_observe_active_glossary` (reads it and drives the router). The call site of `_after_translation_tick` within the streaming loop is **not in the packet** (`omni.py` truncated).
- **Why real:** The docs assert "The generated target window is one routing tick behind the current chunk, so a chunk's own translation cannot influence its own glossary retrieval." That property holds only if `_after_translation_tick` runs *after* `_observe_active_glossary` for the same chunk. If it runs before (or in the same pass that then re-routes), the current chunk's own translation — produced under the currently active glossary — feeds the domain decision for that chunk, closing a self-reinforcing loop with no guardrail. The method was previously a `return None` stub already invoked somewhere, so the call exists; the ordering does not.
- **How to verify:** `grep -n "_after_translation_tick" framework/agents/omni.py` and confirm it is invoked strictly after the per-chunk `_observe_active_glossary`, and that `session.history` at that point holds emitted *target translations* (not source/messages). Neither is confirmable from the packet.
- **Minimal fix direction:** None if ordering is already correct; if not, move the write after routing. Either way, add a test that asserts the current chunk's translation only affects the *next* chunk's `router_text_window`.

# Should fix

### 3. Generated target gets the lenient 2-window "with_text" threshold despite being a self-biased signal
- **Where:** `HybridWindowTopicRouter.observe` — `has_text = router_text and text_source != "none"`; generated_target ⇒ `has_text=True` ⇒ `min_consistent_windows_with_text` (2), and it bypasses the `_audio_probe_guard` (which only fires on `not has_text and has_probe`).
- **Why real:** Source transcript text is domain ground truth; generated target text is produced under the currently active (possibly wrong) glossary and can echo its domain vocabulary. Treating it with the same 2-window, no-raw-evidence-floor path as trusted source text is the weakest point for self-reinforcement the task explicitly flagged. With the renormalization introduced earlier on this branch, a single active text signal renormalizes `conf` toward its top-normalized value, so two windows of generic keyword hits can clear `min_confidence=0.60`.
- **Minimal fix direction:** Give `generated_target` its own (stricter) consistency/confidence treatment distinct from `manifest_source`, or require a raw-evidence floor before a generated-target-only signal can switch.

### 4. Several new Chinese keywords are high-frequency generic words → precision loss, biased toward the default NLP slice
- **Where:** `domain_taxonomy.py` new entries: nlp `注意力|嵌入|预训练|微调|提示` (0.9), `标注|解析|...` (1.0); medicine `试验|...` (1.0).
- **Why real:** `提示` (prompt/hint) and `解析`/`微调` are common in general and medical Chinese ("结果提示…"), and `试验` is generic. Because the default active slice is `nlp_core_10k`, spurious NLP keyword hits combine with the `min_current_margin` guard (which favors staying) to make it harder to *leave* NLP and easier to falsely score NLP on non-NLP audio. No test exercises noisy/realistic Chinese generated text — only one hand-built clean medicine sentence.

# Missing tests / benchmarks
- No agent-level test that a written `router_text_window`/`generated_target` actually flows through `_observe_active_glossary` into a router switch on the *following* chunk (the one-tick-behind contract, item 2).
- No finance/legal generated-target routing test (item 1) — the missing coverage hides that the path is dead there.
- No false-switch/self-reinforcement regression on realistic noisy Chinese generated text (item 3/4); `test_generated_target_chinese_topic_switches_after_two_windows` uses a keyword-dense clean sentence and cannot surface precision loss.
- No test that `session.history` semantics (target vs source) match what `_after_translation_tick` assumes.

# Performance risks
- None material. `_after_translation_tick` is a bounded string join over ≤`window` history items on the CPU path; not a retriever/GPU hot path.

# Spec mismatch / surprise changes
- Docs/README/paper wording present generated-target E2E routing as switching among the domain inventory, but the shipping Chinese-target signal only functions for nlp/medicine (item 1).
- `base_slice: none` + `common_terms type: diagnostic` correctly removes the common base from the active inventory (matches acceptance criteria), and `_active_retrieval_slices` returning only the domain slice is tested. Note `slice_role_for_preset("common_10k")` still returns `"base"` in the registry (`test_common_preset_maps_to_common_terms_slice`) — harmless only because `common_10k` is no longer in the active inventory; it is an internal inconsistency, not a bug in this path.
- Cited eval artifacts (`..._final8.json`) are now host-qualified per AGENTS.md, but are run results not present in the packet and remain unverifiable (pre-existing).

# Possible false positives
- The external-source guard (`current_source not in {"none","generated_target"}`) correctly preserves `manifest_source`/`streaming_asr` and is directly tested (`test_generated_target_translation_does_not_override_external_router_text`); the acceptance criterion "generated target must not override explicit external router_text" is met.
- The current-text dedup (`texts[-1] != current_text`) correctly avoids double-appending when `history` already contains the just-emitted translation; not a bug.
- Dropping the `type=="base"` scan in `_autoterm_base_preset` does not resurrect surprising legacy behavior: with `base_slice` present-and-empty or absent it returns the `"none"` default; `common_terms` is `diagnostic`, so it is never auto-selected as a base.
- `_meta_bool(enable_generated_target_text, True)` defaulting True is intentional and matches the yaml.

# Final recommendation
Do not merge as-is. Before merge: (1) add Chinese finance/legal topic keywords or scope the E2E claim to the covered domains; (2) confirm — with a test — that `_after_translation_tick` runs after per-chunk routing and that `session.history` holds target translations, so the one-tick-behind/no-self-influence property actually holds; (3) treat `generated_target` more conservatively than trusted source text (stricter consistency or a raw-evidence floor) and add a noisy-Chinese false-switch regression. Items 1 (partially), 2, and the `session.history` semantics cannot be fully confirmed from the packet because the `omni.py` call site is truncated.

```

# Verdict
NEEDS_FIX

The change under review is `368472d → 7449b53` (`Add E2E generated-target glossary routing` + `Harden generated-target glossary routing`). It fills in the previously no-op `_after_translation_tick` to write generated target text into `router_text_window`/`router_text_source`, drops `common_terms` from the default active inventory (`base_slice: none`, `type: diagnostic`), simplifies `_autoterm_base_preset`, adds a stricter `min_consistent_windows_generated_target=3` path, and adds Chinese topic keywords for **all four** domains. The prior review's two hardest items (finance/legal Chinese keywords, and lenient 2-window threshold for generated target) are genuinely closed here. What remains are two unverifiable correctness hinges and precision/benchmark gaps.

# Must fix before merge

### 1. The "one routing tick behind" / no-self-influence property is unverifiable from the packet and is the correctness hinge
- **Severity:** High if the call ordering is wrong.
- **Where:** `framework/agents/omni.py` `_after_translation_tick` (writes `router_text_window`) vs `_observe_active_glossary` (reads it). The call site of `_after_translation_tick` inside the streaming/batch loop is **not in the packet** (`omni.py` truncated).
- **Why real:** `docs/adaptive_working_glossary.md` asserts "The generated target window is one routing tick behind the current chunk, so a chunk's own translation cannot influence its own glossary retrieval." That holds only if `_after_translation_tick` runs strictly *after* the per-chunk `_observe_active_glossary`. If it runs before (or in the same routing pass), the current chunk's own translation — produced under the possibly-wrong active glossary — feeds that chunk's domain decision, closing a self-reinforcing loop with no guardrail. The added test `test_generated_target_text_is_used_by_next_router_tick_only` hand-sequences `observe → after_tick → observe`; it proves the flow-through in mock but does **not** prove the production loop orders the two calls that way.
- **How to verify:** `grep -n "_after_translation_tick" framework/agents/omni.py`; confirm it is invoked strictly after the per-chunk `_observe_active_glossary`. Add a test that drives the real per-chunk path and asserts a chunk's translation only affects the *next* chunk's `router_text_window`.
- **Minimal fix direction:** None if ordering is already correct; otherwise move the write after routing.

### 2. `_after_translation_tick` assumes `session.history` holds target translations; this is unconfirmed
- **Severity:** High if `history` holds source/messages.
- **Where:** `_after_translation_tick` — `texts = [... for item in session.history[-window:] ...]`.
- **Why real:** The whole feature depends on `session.history` containing *emitted target translations* (Chinese). If it holds source-side text, message dicts, or interleaved source+target, `text_topic_score` is computed over the wrong content and the generated-target route is silently miscalibrated. `OmniSession.history: List[str]` is declared but what is appended to it is not in the packet.
- **How to verify:** Inspect every `session.history.append(...)` in `omni.py`; confirm it appends the target translation string at the point `_after_translation_tick` reads it, and that the caller's append vs the internal dedup (`texts[-1] != current_text`) don't double-count.

# Should fix

### 3. Several new Chinese keywords are high-frequency/dual-use → precision loss biased toward the default NLP slice
- **Where:** `domain_taxonomy.py` new entries, e.g. nlp `提示|微调|解析` (`提示`="hint/indicate" is common in general and clinical Chinese: "结果提示…"; `解析` is generic), medicine `试验` (generic "trial/experiment"), medicine `核磁|磁共振|CT` marked `case_sensitive=True` (irrelevant for CJK, harmless but sloppy).
- **Why real:** Because the default active slice is `nlp_core_10k`, spurious NLP keyword hits combine with `min_current_margin` (which favors staying) to make it both easier to falsely retain NLP on non-NLP audio and harder to leave. No test exercises noisy/realistic Chinese generated text — only hand-built keyword-dense clean sentences — so precision loss cannot surface.
- **Minimal fix direction:** Drop the most generic tokens or lower their weights; add a noisy-Chinese ACL-only regression asserting `switch_count == 0`.

### 4. Renormalized single-signal confidence still saturates `min_confidence` on the generated-target-only path
- **Where:** `topic_router.py` `_score_hybrid` renormalization (introduced earlier on this branch) + `observe`: `generated_target ⇒ has_text=True`, bypassing `_audio_probe_guard`.
- **Why real:** In the shipping config the generated-target text is often the only active text signal; renormalization drives `conf` toward its top-normalized value, so ~3 windows of generic keyword hits can clear `min_confidence=0.60`. The 3-window consistency guard is the *only* added protection for a signal the task explicitly flags as self-biased; there is no raw-evidence floor as there is for the probe path. Given items 3 and the default NLP bias, this is where a false switch would appear.

# Missing tests / benchmarks
- No test drives the real per-chunk streaming loop to confirm the one-tick-behind contract (item 1) or `session.history` target semantics (item 2).
- No noisy/realistic Chinese generated-target false-switch regression (items 3/4). The four `test_generated_target_chinese_*` tests all use clean keyword-dense single sentences and cannot fail on precision.
- No end-to-end run of the generated-target route exists. All cited artifacts (`..._final8.json`) are router-unit **source-text** diagnostics; the docs themselves say generated-target E2E eval is still future work. Yet the paper wording presents generated-target windows as "the deployable E2E path." The deployable claim is wired but unbenchmarked.

# Performance risks
- None material in this diff. `_after_translation_tick` is a bounded CPU string join over ≤`window` history items, off the retriever/GPU hot path. (The probe re-encode/lock concerns from prior passes live below the review base `368472d` and are out of scope here.)

# Spec mismatch / surprise changes
- `base_slice: none` + `common_terms type: diagnostic` correctly removes the common base from the active inventory and `_active_retrieval_slices` returns only the domain slice (`test_auto_active_retrieval_uses_domain_specific_slice_only`) — matches acceptance criteria. Note the residual inconsistency: `slice_role_for_preset("common_10k")` still returns `"base"` in `slice_registry` (`test_common_preset_maps_to_common_terms_slice`). Harmless only because `common_10k` is no longer in the active inventory; it is an internal inconsistency, not a bug in this path.
- Paper/README wording claims generated-target E2E routing as the shipping route while no E2E evidence exists (see Missing benchmarks).
- `_autoterm_base_preset` no longer scans for `type=="base"`; with `base_slice` present-and-`none` it returns `"none"`, and `common_terms` (now `diagnostic`) is never auto-selected — no resurrected legacy behavior.

# Possible false positives (do not re-raise)
- **The prior Must-fix "finance/legal unreachable for Chinese target" is fixed:** finance/legal Chinese keywords are added, and `_router_all_domains` in `test_hybrid_window_topic_router.py` exercises finance→ and legal→ switches. Do not re-raise as a dead path.
- **The prior Should-fix "generated_target gets lenient 2-window threshold" is fixed:** `min_consistent_windows_generated_target=3` and the `is_generated_target` branch in `observe` apply the stricter path; unit-tested (`..._switches_after_three_windows`).
- The external-source guard (`current_source not in {"none","generated_target"}`) correctly preserves `manifest_source`/`streaming_asr` and is directly tested; the "must not override external router_text" criterion is met.
- The current-text dedup (`texts[-1] != current_text`) correctly avoids double-appending when `history` already holds the just-emitted translation.
- `enable_generated_target_text`/`generated_target_window_chunks`/`generated_target_min_chars` are typed yaml/config fields (not env-var controls), consistent with the workstation constraint.

# Final recommendation
Do not merge as-is. Before merge: (1) confirm — with a test on the real streaming loop, not hand-sequenced method calls — that `_after_translation_tick` runs after per-chunk routing and reads target translations from `session.history`, so the one-tick-behind/no-self-influence property actually holds; (2) add a noisy realistic Chinese generated-target regression asserting zero false switches, and trim the most generic new keywords or give the generated-target-only path a raw-evidence floor rather than relying solely on the 3-window guard; (3) stop presenting generated-target routing as the validated deployable E2E path until an end-to-end run exists, or explicitly scope the claim to "wired, not yet E2E-benchmarked." Items 1 and 2 cannot be fully confirmed from the packet because the `omni.py` call site and `history` append points are truncated.

```text
# Verdict
NEEDS_FIX

The change under review is `368472d → 22fd011` (`Add E2E generated-target glossary routing`, `Harden generated-target glossary routing`, `Document and test generated-target routing guards`). It fills in the previously no-op `_after_translation_tick`, drops `common_terms` from the default active inventory, adds Chinese topic keywords for all four domains, adds a stricter `min_consistent_windows_generated_target=3` path, and adds docs + tests. Several prior-review items are genuinely closed here (finance/legal Chinese keywords now present and tested; stricter generated-target consistency; honest "E2E benchmark pending" caveats). What remains is a real guardrail gap that is the explicit subject of the task, plus test/verification weaknesses on the correctness-critical properties.

# Must fix before merge

### 1. Generated-target routing has no raw-evidence floor; the self-reinforcement guard the task asked for is not actually implemented
- **Severity:** Medium–High (robustness / spec of the feature's whole novelty)
- **Where:** `framework/agents/term_memory/topic_router.py` `HybridWindowTopicRouter.observe` — `is_generated_target` only selects `min_consistent_windows_generated_target` (3); the `_audio_probe_guard` (`not has_text and has_probe`) is bypassed for generated target because `has_text=True`.
- **Why real:** The task explicitly asks "whether using generated target text can self-reinforce wrong glossary choices without enough guardrails." The only added protection over trusted source text is one extra consistency window (3 vs 2). Generated target text is produced under the currently-active (possibly wrong) glossary, so its keyword content is biased toward the current domain. Unlike the audio-only probe path — which requires a raw top-score ≥ 0.50, raw margin ≥ 0.08, and ≥2 positive domains before a renormalized score may switch — the generated-target path has no analogous absolute-evidence floor. Because the branch upstream renormalizes over present signals (documented in `docs/adaptive_working_glossary.md`), a single active text signal can drive `conf` toward its top-normalized value and clear `min_confidence=0.60`, so ~3 windows of biased keyword hits can switch, and `min_current_margin` simultaneously makes it *harder to leave* a wrong initial slice. The dominant realistic failure is sticky retention of the wrong (default `nlp`) slice, which no guard or test addresses.
- **How to verify:** Drive `observe(..., router_text_source="generated_target")` from an `nlp` start with target text that echoes NLP terms while the underlying content is medicine; confirm whether the router can (a) falsely retain nlp or (b) switch on generic biased hits. No such regression exists.
- **Minimal fix direction:** Give `generated_target` an explicit raw-evidence/margin floor before it can reach switch confidence (parallel to `_audio_probe_guard`), and/or add a realistic noisy regression asserting the intended behavior; do not rely solely on the 3-window count.

### 2. The one-tick-behind / no-self-influence property is guaranteed only by a brittle source-substring test
- **Severity:** Medium (correctness hinge, weakly protected)
- **Where:** `test_auto_working_fixed_top10.py::test_streaming_loop_orders_routing_before_generated_target_write`; the actual streaming-loop call sites in `framework/agents/omni.py` are truncated in the packet.
- **Why real:** The docs assert "a chunk's own translation cannot influence its own glossary retrieval," which holds only if `_observe_active_glossary` (inside `_retrieve_batch`) runs before `_after_translation_tick` (inside `_generate_one`/`_generate_batch`) for the same chunk. The added test enforces this via `source.index(...)` string-position comparisons — a structural heuristic that breaks silently on any refactor that reorders code textually without changing runtime order, and cannot observe the actual control flow. It also does not prove `_after_translation_tick` is invoked *only* in the generate path, nor that `session.history` contains only emitted target translations (it is only inferred from `append(text)` preceding `after_translation_tick(text=text)`).
- **How to verify:** Confirm from the untruncated loop that observe precedes after-tick per chunk, and add a runtime test (mock loop) asserting chunk N's translation only affects chunk N+1's `router_text_window` — the hand-sequenced `test_generated_target_text_is_used_by_next_router_tick_only` calls the methods manually and does not exercise the loop.
- **Minimal fix direction:** Add a mock end-to-end streaming assertion; keep the string test only as a supplement.

# Should fix

- **`session.history` content semantics unconfirmed.** `_after_translation_tick` reads `session.history[-window:]` as generated target text. If history is appended anywhere outside the generate path with source/message content, `text_topic_score` is computed over the wrong content. Only inferred from the two generate-path appends; verify no other `session.history.append` interleaves non-translation strings.
- **`slice_role_for_preset("common_10k")` still returns `"base"`** (`test_common_preset_maps_to_common_terms_slice`) while the config marks `common_terms` `type: diagnostic` and drops it from the active inventory. Harmless in the active path but an internal inconsistency now that `base_slice: none`.
- **`核磁|磁共振|CT` medicine keyword:** `CT` in a CJK regex has no word boundary and matches any substring; on mixed-language target text it can match inside unrelated tokens. Low impact (target is Chinese) but sloppy for a case-insensitive bare `CT`.

# Missing tests / benchmarks
- No realistic noisy/self-reinforcement regression for generated target (item 1). The four `test_generated_target_chinese_*` tests all use clean keyword-dense single sentences; the sole noise test (`..._noisy_generic_chinese_does_not_switch_to_nlp`) is one generic sentence checking non-switch, not a wrong-glossary bias case.
- No runtime streaming-loop test of the one-tick-behind contract (item 2).
- No end-to-end generated-target switch-quality run exists; the docs themselves now state this is pending. Cited `..._final8.json` artifacts are source-text router-unit diagnostics, correctly labeled as upper bounds.

# Performance risks
- None material in this diff. `_after_translation_tick` is a bounded CPU string join over ≤`window` history items, off the retriever/GPU path. No TP/PP, scheduling, or cache interaction. (Probe re-encode/lock concerns from earlier reviews live below base `368472d` and are out of scope.)

# Spec mismatch / surprise changes
- `base_slice: none` + `common_terms type: diagnostic` correctly removes the common base; `_active_retrieval_slices` returning only the domain slice is tested (`test_auto_active_retrieval_uses_domain_specific_slice_only`). `_autoterm_base_preset` no longer scans for `type=="base"`; with `base_slice` present-and-`none` it returns `"none"`, and `common_terms` (diagnostic) is never auto-selected — no resurrected legacy behavior. Matches acceptance criteria.
- README/paper wording presents the generated-target route as "the wired production path" but is now appropriately caveated ("End-to-end generated-target benchmarking is still pending"; "Full E2E generated-target switch quality remains a pending benchmark"). This is honest, but note the shipping primary signal is generated target (no ASR), and audio-only probe switching remains effectively inert on real audio given `audio_probe_min_raw_margin=0.08` vs the ~0.01 real deltas the repo's own probe doc reports — so the initial slice dominates until translations accumulate.

# Possible false positives (do not re-raise)
- The prior "finance/legal unreachable for Chinese target" is fixed: Chinese finance/legal keywords added and exercised by `_router_all_domains` finance/legal switch tests.
- The prior "generated_target gets lenient 2-window threshold" is fixed: `min_consistent_windows_generated_target=3` plumbed yaml → `OmniConfig` → `RouterConfig` and unit-tested.
- The external-source guard (`current_source not in {"none","generated_target"}`) correctly preserves `manifest_source`/`streaming_asr` and is directly tested — acceptance criterion "must not override external router_text" met.
- The current-text dedup (`texts[-1] != current_text`) correctly avoids double-appending when history already holds the just-emitted translation.
- `enable_generated_target_text`/`generated_target_window_chunks`/`generated_target_min_chars` are typed yaml/config fields (not env-var controls), consistent with the workstation constraint.
- The generic Chinese tokens flagged in an earlier packet (`提示`/`解析`) are **not** present in this HEAD's `domain_taxonomy.py` diff; do not re-raise them.

# Final recommendation
Do not merge as-is. Before merge: (1) add a real guardrail for the generated-target-only path — an absolute raw-evidence/margin floor analogous to `_audio_probe_guard`, not just the 3-window count — since a stricter consistency count alone does not answer the task's explicit self-reinforcement question; (2) add a mock streaming-loop test that proves the one-tick-behind property at runtime and confirm `session.history` holds only target translations, rather than relying on the brittle source-substring ordering test; (3) add a realistic noisy/wrong-glossary Chinese generated-target regression. Items depending on the truncated `omni.py` streaming loop (exact observe/after-tick ordering and `history` append sites) cannot be fully confirmed from the packet.

```

Current file excerpt/full content, possibly truncated:
```text
# Verdict
NEEDS_FIX

The router change (`has_text_topic_signal`) is small, targeted, and its stated fix is confirmed by the new unit test. But the benchmark that headlines this branch is driven by an oracle probe over gold reference text, so its central metrics are near-vacuous; the router change also silently alters a second, unguarded code path; and the new doc violates AGENTS path rules. The unit tests pass (17/17 per the log), but the reported 64-window/full-window JSON numbers are Taurus-only and not in the packet.

# Must fix before merge

### 1. Benchmark cannot detect the failure modes the task asks about (oracle probe + gold-reference proxy)
- **Severity:** Medium–High (benchmark validity / spec mismatch)
- **Where:** `eval/streaming_sst/eval_mixed_domain_switch.py` `probe_for_domain` (fed via `evaluate_playlist` with `probe_mode == "expected"`); `read_acl_blocks`/`read_medicine_blocks` window text.
- **Why real:**
  - `probe_for_domain(block.expected_domain)` always returns the *correct* domain at a fixed clean margin (0.35 vs 0.08). Every switch decision is therefore steered by an oracle that is never wrong. Consequently `wrong_switch_count == 0`, `steady_state_accuracy == 1.0`, and `regression_pass == true` are structurally guaranteed, not evidence that routing discriminates domains. The task explicitly asks to check "whether auto glossary routing can switch between NLP and medicine domains" and to not "hide wrong-domain steady-state behavior" — but with an always-correct probe there is no wrong-domain behavior to hide, so the metric is uninformative rather than validated.
  - The window text is ACL Chinese *target segments* and RASST medicine Chinese *references* — human gold translations, not model output produced under a possibly-wrong active glossary. This removes exactly the self-reinforcement risk repeatedly flagged in the branch's own prior reviews (`.codex/reviews/claude-review-20260706-234102.md` Must-fix #1). The proxy is therefore optimistic.
  - The doc `docs/auto_glossary_mixed_switch_20260707.md` `结论` states the router "可以...稳定切换...稳定" without inline caveat that this holds only under a per-block oracle probe; the mid-doc labeling ("probe_mode=expected 表示...可控期望域证据") is present but the headline conclusion and the `adaptive_working_glossary_eval.md` addition overstate it.
- **How to verify:** Add a `probe_mode` variant that feeds contested/noisy multi-domain probe scores (wrong domain occasionally higher, margins near the `generated_target_probe_min_raw_margin=0.01` floor) and confirm whether `wrong_switch_count` can become nonzero; grep `probe_for_domain` to confirm it is keyed off `block.expected_domain` (it is).
- **Minimal fix direction:** Either add a noisy/contested-probe scenario and report it, or restate the doc conclusion as "state-machine switches correctly *given* oracle domain-probe evidence," making explicit that domain discrimination and self-reinforcement are untested by this proxy.

### 2. `_score_hybrid` now renormalizes on `has_text_topic_signal` while `observe` still gates on `has_text` — reopens the probe-saturates-confidence path for text-present/topic-empty windows without a raw-evidence floor
- **Severity:** Medium (hidden cross-path robustness regression)
- **Where:** `framework/agents/term_memory/topic_router.py` — new `has_text_topic_signal` used in `active_weight_sum`, the weighted sum, and `alpha` (diff hunks @764/@780/@796/@807); the `observe` guard chain still computes its own `has_text` and only triggers `_audio_probe_guard` on `not has_text and has_probe`.
- **Why real:** For a `manifest_source`/`streaming_asr` window whose text has zero topic-keyword hits (`has_text_topic_signal=False`) but a probe present, the confidence is now renormalized over probe-only weight (denominator collapses to the probe weight), driving `conf` toward the normalized probe top — the exact saturation `_audio_probe_guard` (floors 0.50/0.08/2) was added to prevent. But because `observe` still sees `has_text=True`, the audio-probe guard branch is skipped and only the 2-window `min_consistent_windows_with_text` applies. `generated_target` is protected by `_generated_target_probe_guard`, but its floors are lenient (top 0.25, margin 0.01), so a weak/contested probe on generic generated text can also clear it. The new unit test uses the clean oracle probe (0.35/0.08) and cannot surface this.
- **How to verify:** Drive `observe(..., router_text=<generic text, no keyword hits>, router_text_source="manifest_source", domain_probe_scores=<contested probe, medicine 0.30 vs nlp 0.28>)` over ≥2 windows under production weights (`min_confidence=0.60`) and check for a switch with no raw-evidence floor; repeat with `generated_target` and a probe just above the 0.25/0.01 floor.
- **Minimal fix direction:** Reconcile the two definitions — either apply an absolute-evidence floor whenever the *effective* signal is probe-only (regardless of `has_text`), or route the `has_text && !has_text_topic_signal` case through the same guard as audio-only. Add a contested-probe regression asserting no false switch.

# Should fix

### 3. New doc violates AGENTS path rules and is non-reproducible
- **Where:** `docs/auto_glossary_mixed_switch_20260707.md` — `Taurus checkout: /home/jiaxuanluo/rasst-demo`, output dir `/mnt/data1/jiaxuanluo/rasst_eval/...`, and command blocks `cd /home/jiaxuanluo/rasst-demo`.
- **Why real:** AGENTS.md requires host-qualified Taurus paths and forbids bare `/home/...`; it also asks new artifacts to live under `/mnt/taurus/data2/jiaxuanluo`. The script's own defaults (`DEFAULT_MEDICINE_TEXT_DIR = /mnt/taurus/data2/...`) are compliant, so the doc commands are inconsistent with the code and not reproducible as written. Prior passes on this branch fixed this exact class of issue; this doc reintroduces it.
- **Minimal fix direction:** Host-qualify the doc paths (`/mnt/taurus/home/...`, `/mnt/taurus/data2/...`) to match the script.

# Missing tests / benchmarks
- No regression for the path change in Must-fix #2: no test that generic `manifest_source` text + a contested/weak probe does not false-switch, and none that generic `generated_target` text + a probe just above the lenient floor is correctly refused.
- No test/benchmark with a wrong or noisy probe; every reported "pass" (`wrong_switch_count=0`, `steady_state=1.0`) is against an always-correct probe, so it cannot fail on discrimination.
- The reported 64-window and 1905-window JSON results (`0.9719`, `0.9906`, etc.) are described only in `.codex/claude-log-mixed-switch.md`; the JSON artifacts are not in the packet, so those specific numbers are unverifiable (expected under AGENTS, but note it).

# Performance risks
- None material. The change is CPU-side scalar/weight bookkeeping in `_score_hybrid`; the benchmark drives the router in-process with hysteresis disabled and no retriever/GPU path. No TP/PP, scheduling, or cache interaction.

# Spec mismatch / surprise changes
- Benchmark presents an oracle-probe, gold-reference proxy as validation of domain switching (Must-fix #1); the "no-probe diagnostic fails" row only re-confirms that `_generated_target_probe_guard` blocks without probe evidence — it does not show target text alone identifies the domain.
- `_score_hybrid` weight/alpha semantics changed for the topically-empty text case (audio EMA alpha now used, guard-less probe renormalization); documented behavior of the fixed-weight formula for `manifest_source`/`streaming_asr` is silently altered (Must-fix #2).
- Benchmark disables warmup/update/cooldown; "max latency = 3" is windows, not deployment latency. Mid-doc labels it a proxy, but the headline `结论` does not repeat the caveat.

# Possible false positives (do not re-raise)
- The `has_text_topic_signal` change does **not** affect keyword-dense text (`manifest_source`/`generated_target` with hits): `has_text_topic_signal` is then True, identical to the old `has_text` behavior; existing tests (`test_acl_to_medicine_switches_after_two_text_windows`, the four `test_generated_target_chinese_*`, `test_metadata_prior_...`) still pass per the log.
- `generated_target` still requires `_generated_target_probe_guard`, so the "generic text switches" behavior in the new test is not fully unguarded — the concern in Must-fix #2 is the lenient floor and the guard-less `manifest_source`/`streaming_asr` sub-case, not the generated-target oracle test.
- `.codex/` (task files, prior reviews, packets) is untracked (`?? .codex/`) and not part of commits `b96b982`/`1e82762`; the diff stat touches only the 6 real files, so this is not an AGENTS "commit generated dumps" violation as-is.
- Transition grace = `max_switch_windows` (3) exactly covers the 2 lagging wrong windows per passing transition; the arithmetic (640×0.9719 ⇒ 18 wrong = 9 transitions × 2) is consistent and does not hide steady-state error.

# Final recommendation
Do not merge as-is. Before merge: (1) stop presenting the oracle-probe/gold-reference run as demonstrating domain switching — add a contested/noisy-probe scenario or restate the conclusion as "state machine given correct probe evidence"; (2) reconcile `has_text` vs `has_text_topic_signal` so a probe-only-effective window cannot clear `min_confidence` without a raw-evidence floor on the `manifest_source`/`streaming_asr` path, and add the corresponding negative test; (3) host-qualify the new doc's paths per AGENTS. The core router edit is correct for keyword-bearing text; the risk is entirely in the topically-empty sub-case and in the benchmark's evidentiary weight.

# Verdict
NEEDS_FIX

The router edit (`has_text_topic_signal`) does close the specific dilution weakness it targets and the new unit tests confirm that narrow case. But the same edit silently changes the renormalization denominator on a second, unguarded code path, reintroducing a probe-free false-switch route; and the headline benchmark's "pass" numbers are structurally produced by a per-block oracle probe, so they do not demonstrate the domain discrimination the task asks about. The deployable `generated_target` path is safe; the regression is on the `manifest_source`/`streaming_asr` routes and is not covered by the benchmark (which never supplies query embeddings) or any test.

Evidence bounds: the four `_score_hybrid` hunks (@764/@785/@801/@812) and the `observe` guard hunk (@596) are shown, so Finding A rests on shown code. `_normalize_score_map`, the full `_probe_guard`, and the JSON artifacts are truncated/absent; the 640/1905-window numbers are Taurus-only and unverifiable from the packet.

# Must fix before merge

### 1. `has_text_topic_signal` collapses the renormalization denominator on the text-present/topic-empty path, letting a lone speech centroid saturate `min_confidence`
- **Severity:** High (hidden cross-path regression; directly touches the "text alone must not switch without probe" acceptance criterion, on a non-`generated_target` source)
- **Where:** `framework/agents/term_memory/topic_router.py` `_score_hybrid` — `active_weight_sum` (@785), the weighted sum (@801/@812), and `alpha` (@812) now key off `has_text_topic_signal` instead of `has_text`; `observe`'s new guard (@596) only fires on `has_probe and has_text and not has_text_topic_signal`.
- **Why real:** For a `manifest_source`/`streaming_asr` window whose text has zero topic-keyword hits (`has_text_topic_signal=False`), no probe (`has_probe=False`), but a query embedding / EMA centroid present:
  - **Before:** `has_text=True` kept `text_topic_weight` (0.60) in `active_weight_sum`; with `text_score=0` for all domains, `conf = 0.10·centroid / (0.60+0.10) ≈ 0.14·centroid < 0.60` → blocked by `min_confidence`.
  - **After:** text weight is removed from the denominator, so `conf = 0.10·centroid / 0.10 = centroid_normalized`, which saturates toward ~1.0 and clears `min_confidence=0.60`. The new `probe_only_evidence_insufficient` guard is gated on `has_probe`, so this centroid-only, no-probe sub-case falls straight through to the confidence check and can switch after `min_consistent_windows_with_text=2`. The docs' own probe note calls the centroid non-discriminative, so this is a likely false switch, and it happens with **no probe evidence at all** — the opposite of what the guard was added to enforce.
- **How to verify:** `observe(state, query_embedding=<wrong-domain vector>, [], now_s=k, router_text="<generic text, no keyword hits>", router_text_source="manifest_source", domain_probe_scores={})` over 2 windows under the shipped weights (`min_confidence=0.60`); confirm a switch fires post-change and did not pre-change. Note the mixed-switch benchmark cannot surface this: `evaluate_playlist` always calls `router.observe(..., None, ...)` (query_embedding=None → `has_embedding=False`), so `active_weight_sum` is 0 in the no-probe row and no switch occurs.
- **Minimal fix direction:** Apply the raw-evidence floor whenever the *effective* signal degrades to a single renormalized signal — route `has_text and not has_text_topic_signal` (regardless of `has_probe`) through the same absolute-evidence guard as the audio-only path, or block a lone renormalized centroid from reaching switch confidence. Add the corresponding negative test.

# Should fix

### 2. Benchmark "pass" is steered by a per-block oracle probe; expected-mode results don't demonstrate domain discrimination
- **Severity:** Medium (benchmark validity)
- **Where:** `eval/streaming_sst/eval_mixed_domain_switch.py` `probe_for_domain(block.expected_domain, mode="expected")`; window text is ACL gold target segments + medicine gold references.
- **Why real:** In `expected` mode the probe is always the correct domain at a fixed clean margin (0.90 vs 0.35), fed from the very first window of each new block. `wrong_switch_count=0`, `steady_state_accuracy=1.0`, `regression_pass=true` are therefore near-structural, and the `inverted` row (probe wrong ⇒ 10 wrong switches) confirms the *probe* dominates the decision — so the correct outcomes in `expected` mode are probe-driven, not evidence that target text (or real MaxSim audio) discriminates domains. The gold references also remove the self-reinforcement risk that a model-generated target would carry. The doc's second paragraph now caveats this ("不证明真实 speech domain probe 的域判别质量"), which is a genuine mitigation over the prior pass, but the `结论` and the `adaptive_working_glossary_eval.md` addition still read as a capability claim ("稳定切换").
- **Minimal fix direction:** State the conclusion as "state machine switches correctly *given* clean probe evidence"; do not present the oracle-probe/gold-reference run as evidence of domain discrimination or self-reinforcement resistance.

### 3. Data provenance / path deviations
- `DEFAULT_ACL_ROOT` (`.../acl6060_zh_segments/segments.target`, `segments.meta.jsonl`) and `DEFAULT_MEDICINE_TEXT_DIR` (`/mnt/taurus/data2/jiaxuanluo/RASST/...`) differ from AGENTS' canonical RASST path (`/mnt/data2/jiaxuanluo/RASST`) and from the prior eval script's smoke paths; how `segments.target`/`segments.meta.jsonl` were produced is undocumented, so the run is not reproducible from the packet.
- The doc stages outputs under `/mnt/taurus/data1/...`; AGENTS prefers `/mnt/taurus/data2/jiaxuanluo` for new artifacts. Host-qualified now (prior complaint addressed), but data1 vs data2 is a soft deviation.
- `read_acl_blocks` filters `text_lines` for non-empty but indexes `meta` by raw enumerate `idx`; if either file contains blank lines, talk-grouping (block boundaries, hence transition counts) can misalign. Data-dependent, unverifiable here.

# Missing tests / benchmarks
- No test for Finding A: generic `manifest_source`/`streaming_asr` text + wrong-domain centroid + no probe must not switch. This is the exact sub-case the new gating opened and no test drives query embeddings.
- No non-oracle probe run: every reported `regression_pass=true` uses an always-correct probe, so it cannot fail on discrimination. The `contested`/`inverted` rows are diagnostics of probe *presence*, not of text/audio discrimination.
- The 640/1905-window JSON results live only in `.codex/claude-log-mixed-switch.md`; artifacts are not in the packet, so the specific numbers are unverifiable.

# Performance risks
None material. The change is CPU-side scalar/weight bookkeeping in `_score_hybrid`; the benchmark runs the router in-process with hysteresis disabled and no retriever/GPU, TP/PP, scheduling, or cache path.

# Spec mismatch / surprise changes
- `_score_hybrid` weight/`alpha` semantics silently change for the topically-empty text case (`manifest_source`/`streaming_asr`): text weight dropped from the denominator, `audio_ema_alpha` used instead of `text_ema_alpha`. The docs describe the fixed-weight formula and the audio-probe floor but not this sub-case (Finding A).
- Benchmark presents an oracle-probe/gold-reference proxy; the `no-probe` row only re-confirms `generated_target_probe_guard` blocks without probe evidence — it does not show target text alone identifies the domain (Finding 2).

# Possible false positives (do not re-raise)
- The `generated_target` deployable path is **not** affected by Finding A: it is blocked at the prior branch (`generated_target_probe_evidence_insufficient`) whenever probe evidence is absent (`min_positive_domains=1`), so a probe-free generated-target window cannot reach the renormalized confidence check.
- For keyword-bearing text (`has_text_topic_signal=True`), the change is identical to the old `has_text` behavior; the existing `test_generated_target_chinese_*` / `test_acl_to_medicine_*` / `test_metadata_prior_*` cases are unaffected (20/20 pass per the log).
- The transition grace window equals `max_switch_windows` (3), which exactly covers the ≤3-window consistency lag; a switch slower than 3 windows fails the transition and its excess wrong windows count in steady-state — so the grace design does not hide steady-state error (acceptance criterion met on this point).
- `.codex/` is untracked (`?? .codex/`) and not part of the 4 reviewed commits; the diff stat touches only the 6 tracked files, so it is not an AGENTS "commit generated dumps" violation.
- `build_schedule` uses a locally seeded `random.Random(seed)`; random-schedule reproducibility is fine.

# Final recommendation
Do not merge as-is. (1) Reconcile `has_text` vs `has_text_topic_signal` so a window whose *effective* evidence is a single renormalized signal — centroid or probe — cannot clear `min_confidence` without an absolute-evidence floor, and add the negative test for the `manifest_source`/`streaming_asr` + centroid + no-probe case. (2) Restate the benchmark conclusion as "state machine given clean probe evidence," not domain discrimination, since every `expected`-mode pass is oracle-steered. (3) Document/align the new default data paths and prefer `/mnt/taurus/data2` per AGENTS. The narrow dilution fix and its unit tests are correct; the risk is the untested topic-empty sub-case and the benchmark's evidentiary weight.

## .codex/reviews/claude-review-20260707-015058.md

Current file excerpt/full content, possibly truncated:
```text
# Verdict
NEEDS_FIX

The reviewed change (43f2b34 → fccba73) is additive: one streaming harness, one unit-test file, and doc/TODO updates. It correctly does **not** claim E2E evidence — the TODO table marks real replay `blocked` and the log records only a dry-run. That part matches the acceptance criteria. But the harness's entire scoring pipeline depends on runtime-server metadata fields whose existence I cannot confirm from the packet, and the one field that anchors all domain/latency scoring silently falls back to a fabricated value when absent. When this harness is eventually run, it will likely produce plausible-but-meaningless numbers without erroring. The `.codex/` tree is untracked and out of scope.

# Must fix before merge

### 1. `cursor_samples` fallback silently fabricates audio-position alignment
- **Severity:** High (benchmark validity)
- **Where:** `eval/streaming_sst/eval_mixed_audio_switch.py` `run_streaming_eval`, `cursor_samples = int(meta.get("cursor_samples") or (events_seen * chunk_samples))`.
- **Why real:** Every downstream metric — `expected_domain_at`, `domain_transitions` (boundary crossing, `latency_events`, `latency_s`), steady-state accuracy, probe accuracy — is keyed off `cursor_samples`. If the server does not emit `meta.cursor_samples`, the code substitutes `events_seen * chunk_samples`. `events_seen` counts *partial events*, not audio chunks fed; the server emits partials on its own generation cadence (typically one per `latency_multiplier` segments, not one per sent chunk), so this product has no relationship to the true audio cursor. The whole playlist-span alignment then drifts monotonically and the reported switch latencies / steady-state accuracy are noise. Critically, the documented JSON event schema in `docs/adaptive_working_glossary.md` (in this packet) lists `topic`, `topic_router`, `domain_probe_scores`, `retrieve_s` — but **not** `cursor_samples`, so the fallback is the *likely* path, not the edge case. A legitimate `cursor_samples == 0` on the first event also wrongly triggers the fallback (`0 or ...`).
- **How to verify:** Grep the server/omni JSON-WS metadata emission for `cursor_samples`; run one short real chunk against `127.0.0.1:8011` and inspect whether `meta.cursor_samples` is present and monotonically increases with fed samples.
- **Minimal fix direction:** Require `cursor_samples` explicitly (`meta.get("cursor_samples")` is `None` → raise / record a hard failure), or track cursor on the *feed* side (bytes actually sent) instead of deriving it from event count. Do not silently substitute an event-count proxy.

# Should fix

### 2. Metric extraction assumes an unverified server-metadata contract and degrades silently
- **Where:** `run_streaming_eval` record construction: `router.get("to_domain") or router.get("target_domain")`, `meta.get("router_text_source")`, `meta.get("candidate_pool_count")`, `meta.get("fixed_prompt_k")`, `topic.get("active_domain")`, etc.
- **Why real:** Only `topic.active_domain`, `topic.active_glossary_preset`, `topic.switch_count`, `topic_router.action`, `domain_probe_scores`, `retrieve_s`, `domain_probe_s` are corroborated by the documented schema. If `to_domain`/`target_domain`, `router_text_source`, `candidate_pool_count`, or `cursor_samples` are named differently server-side, each defaults to `""`/`0` and `wrong_switch_count` is undercounted (the `and item.get("router_target_domain")` filter drops empties), `router_text_sources`/candidate-count diagnostics become empty — with `regression_pass` still able to read `true`. None of this fails loudly. The tests never exercise this mapping (see Missing tests).
- **Minimal fix direction:** Assert the required meta keys exist on the first real partial and error out on the schema mismatch, rather than defaulting.

### 3. Sole run-termination is a single 60 s idle timeout — fragile for the intended 4.68 h run
- **Where:** `run_streaming_eval` `idle = 0; while idle < 1: ... except asyncio.TimeoutError: idle += 1`.
- **Why real:** The loop exits on the *first* 60 s gap with no message. For a ~4.68 h real playlist with model-generation overhead and variable per-segment latency, a >60 s stall mid-stream would exit early, truncate `records`, and mark later transitions as failed. There is no completion/EOF-final-event detection (only `type == "partial"` is counted). After early exit, `await feed_task` keeps sending audio while nothing reads the socket, and `max_size=None` gives the client an unbounded receive buffer.
- **Minimal fix direction:** Terminate on an explicit server end/complete event and/or a bounded idle count after EOF; cancel/await `feed_task` deterministically.

### 4. Audio wire-format is unverified
- **Where:** `feed()` sends `chunk.tobytes()` where `chunk` is `float32` in [-1,1) (`read_wav` divides int16 by 32768). If the JSON-WS input path expects int16 PCM, every byte is misinterpreted. Not confirmable from the packet.
- **Minimal fix direction:** Confirm the server's expected PCM dtype against the existing `eval_auto_glossary.py` audio path and match it explicitly.

### 5. `read_acl_audio_blocks` applies `limit_items` before file-existence filtering
- **Where:** `list(by_talk.items())[: limit_items]` then `selected = [p for p in selected if Path(p).is_file()]`; a block with zero existing files is dropped.
- **Why real:** If any of the first `limit_items` talks has missing wavs, you silently get fewer than the intended 5 ACL blocks (or 0), changing playlist length/transition count without warning. The dry-run happening to find 5 blocks does not guarantee this on other checkouts.
- **Minimal fix direction:** Filter for existence first, then take `limit_items`.

### 6. Minor / AGENTS
- Doc stages outputs under `/mnt/taurus/data1/...`; AGENTS prefers `/mnt/taurus/data2/jiaxuanluo` for new artifacts (host-qualified, so soft deviation only — prior passes flagged the same class).
- `import statistics` is unused (dead import).

# Missing tests / benchmarks
- No test covers `run_streaming_eval` or the `meta` → record extraction mapping — i.e., the exact code that reads `cursor_samples`, `to_domain`, `router_text_source`, etc. The three unit tests only feed hand-built `records` dicts into the pure scoring functions, so a wrong/absent server field name or the `cursor_samples` fallback (Must-fix #1) cannot be caught.
- No test drives the fallback path or asserts behavior when `cursor_samples` is missing.
- `probe_top_accuracy`/steady-state are asserted only on clean, hand-constructed records; no contested/mismatched-probe case (acceptable given this is a harness, but the discrimination claims will rest on the untested real path).
- The reported dry-run block list / `16,848.115 s` figure lives only in `.codex/claude-log-mixed-audio.md`; the JSON artifacts are Taurus-only and not in the packet, so those numbers are unverifiable here (expected under AGENTS, noted).

# Performance risks
- None material on the serving hot path; the harness is client-side. Note the intended real run is ~4.68 h of audio; combined with Should-fix #3 (unbounded `max_size=None` buffer, no realtime pacing at `feed_sleep=0`) a long run can accumulate client-side memory if reads stall. `iter_pcm_chunks` also `np.concatenate`s a carry across every block boundary — negligible.

# Spec mismatch / surprise changes
- TODO table row "Real mixed-audio harness → done (dry-run verified)" is accurate; "Real speech-window domain-probe replay → blocked" and "Full E2E … pending" correctly avoid overclaiming. No E2E evidence is asserted, satisfying "should not claim full E2E evidence before a valid `hybrid_window_topic` server run." The harness reads `meta.domain_probe_scores` (routing-only), consistent with "do not use ASR/source transcript text as routing evidence."
- No new env-var controls; all knobs are CLI flags. Matches the workstation/AGENTS constraint.

# Possible false positives (do not re-raise)
- `build_schedule` random path uses a locally seeded `random.Random(seed)` — reproducible; not a bug.
- The transition grace window (`transition_grace_events`) is bounded by `max_switch_events` and keyed off the first correct-active event; a transition that never reaches the target gets no grace and its wrong windows count in steady-state, so grace does not hide steady-state error.
- `.codex/` is untracked (`?? .codex/`) and not part of commits b693168/fccba73; the diff stat touches only the 3 tracked files, so this is not an AGENTS "commit generated dumps" violation.
- The dry-run needing the actual audio files present is expected — it is the path/span discovery validation the criteria asked for, and it does not require a GPU.

# Final recommendation
Do not merge as-is. Before merge: (1) make `cursor_samples` a hard requirement or derive the cursor from bytes fed, so span alignment cannot be silently fabricated; (2) assert the required `meta`/`topic`/`topic_router` field names on the first real partial instead of defaulting to empty; (3) replace the single-60 s-idle termination with explicit completion detection for the long real run; and (4) confirm the PCM wire dtype and fix the ACL block-limit-before-existence ordering. The pure scoring functions and their unit tests are sound; the risk is entirely in the untested live-WS extraction path and its silent-degradation defaults, none of which the current tests can catch.

```

User request and acceptance criteria:

- Continue through the remaining auto-term TODO checklist.

## Context: AGENTS.md

```text
# RASST-Demo Agent Instructions

This repository is the demo-system continuation of the previous InfiniSST
EMNLP System Demonstration draft. The current working name is `rasst-demo`.
Treat it as a live demo project for retrieval-aware, terminology-sensitive
streaming speech translation, not as a generic InfiniSST archive.

## Communication

- Prefer English for user-facing explanations unless Chinese is clearly faster,
  more precise, or requested.
- If the user's English or mixed English/Chinese wording is unnatural,
  ambiguous, or unprofessional, include a concise `Better English:` correction.
- Keep language feedback separate from engineering work.
- If an instruction is ambiguous enough to affect paths, code, experiments, or
  paper claims, ask a targeted clarification question before acting.

## Canonical Paths

- Repo root: `/mnt/taurus/home/jiaxuanluo/rasst-demo`
- Demo paper draft: `/mnt/taurus/home/jiaxuanluo/rasst-demo/demo_paper_emnlp`
- Main RASST reference: `/mnt/data2/jiaxuanluo/RASST`
- User-expected RASST home path, if later symlinked or moved:
  `/mnt/taurus/home/jiaxuanluo/RASST`
- Optional RL/post-training reference: `/mnt/taurus/home/jiaxuanluo/RAPO`

Use host-qualified Taurus paths in scripts, docs, and reports. Do not write new
commands using bare `/home/...` or Aries-only `/mnt/aries/...` paths unless the
task explicitly concerns Aries storage.

Large generated files, model checkpoints, logs, recordings, and benchmark dumps
should stay out of the repo unless the user explicitly asks to commit or package
them. Prefer a separate runtime/data root under `/mnt/taurus/data2/jiaxuanluo`
for new large artifacts.

## Current Demo Scope

The baseline system is an InfiniSST-style multi-user simultaneous speech
translation demo with:

- web and Electron frontends;
- microphone, file, YouTube/web, and desktop system-audio input paths;
- a scheduler/back-end split for concurrent sessions;
- prefill/decode batching, KV-cache reuse, attention-sink/sliding-window
  inference, and paged attention support;
- prior 32-sessions-per-GPU positioning from the old draft.

For a new demo-track submission, do not rely on "long speech translation with an
LLM" or "32 sessions per GPU" as the main novelty. Treat those as baseline
system strengths. The refreshed claim should focus on term-dense vertical-domain
translation: domain glossary retrieval, live terminology control, term-recall
diagnostics, and a demo experience that makes terminology corrections visible.

## Extension Direction

Prioritize a practical RASST-Demo story:

```text
streaming speech -> candidate terms/retrieved evidence -> terminology-aware
translation -> live UI diagnostics for latency, term recall, and corrections
```

Good demo features include:

- domain or glossary selection for medical, legal, academic, or financial
  speech;
- live display of retrieved terms/evidence next to the translation;
- user-visible term correction or acceptance controls;
- per-session diagnostics for latency, throughput, term recall, and false-copy
  behavior;
- comparison between plain InfiniSST and terminology-aware/RAG modes.

Avoid making RL the core demo requirement unless experiments already show a
clear user-facing win. RAPO-style RL/post-training is optional and should be
framed as a low-latency 4B student or adaptive policy extension. A 30B model can
remain the stronger teacher, reference model, or quality baseline when that is
more compelling for a demo.

## Relationship To RAPO

RAPO is a post-training reference, not the main identity of this demo repo. If
used, frame RAPO-style work as optional retrieval-aware or terminology-aware
post-training for a smaller student model.

The Speech LLM is the agent. Terminology retrieval, glossary lookup, or domain
evidence is a tool/evidence source. DPO, SimPO, GRPO, and OPD are training
backends; they are not the demo contribution by themselves.

For a compute-conscious extension, prefer:

```text
30B RASST/Qwen-Omni system as demo engine or teacher
4B student as low-latency optional variant
offline teacher/rubric feedback for term recall, false-copy behavior, latency,
and correction quality
```

Do not plan full 30B online GRPO unless the user explicitly changes the scope.

## Paper Framing

The paper in `demo_paper_emnlp` is a starting point, not a final submission.
When revising it:

- update the title away from pure high-throughput InfiniSST scheduling if the
  demo is now RASST/terminology centered;
- keep the 32-session scheduling result as a systems capability, not the whole
  contribution;
- add concrete evaluation, because EMNLP demo submissions can be desk rejected
  if they report no evaluation;
- include screenshots or diagrams of the actual updated demo;
- include a live demo link or installable package plan;
- keep the submission within the current demo-track page limit and style rules;
- state licensing and deployment constraints clearly.

The likely contribution shape is:

1. an interactive streaming speech translation demo for term-dense domains;
2. retrieval-aware terminology assistance integrated into a low-latency SST UI;
3. system evidence showing the quality-latency-terminology trade-off under
   concurrent use.

## Engineering Rules

- Read the existing code before editing; this repo contains a web server,
  Electron app, model wrappers, scheduler, and paper draft.
- Keep changes scoped to the demo path unless the user explicitly asks to sync
  with another repo.
- Prefer small smoke tests before reporting success.
- After committing material code, config, docs, evaluation summaries, or
  progress records, push the branch to the GitHub remote before reporting the
  task complete unless the user explicitly says not to push. Local-only commits
  are not a source of truth for this project.
- Do not commit generated logs, caches, model weights, downloaded checkpoints,
  large media, or temporary LaTeX build products.
- If borrowing code from InfiniSST, RASST, or RAPO, record the source path and
  keep the demo-facing behavior clear.

## Useful Entry Points

- Backend API: `serve/api.py`
- Inference engine: `serve/inference_engine.py`
- Scheduler: `serve/scheduler.py`
- Main agents: `agents/infinisst.py`, `agents/infinisst_fast.py`,
  `agents/infinisst_faster.py`
- Web/static frontend: `serve/static/`
- Electron frontend: `electron/`
- Old demo paper: `demo_paper_emnlp/latex/`
- Integration tests: `test_integrated_system.py`, `test_scheduler_system.py`

When evaluating submission readiness, inspect both the runnable demo and the
paper draft. The submission should be judged by what a reviewer can see in the
live demo/video, not only by model-training claims.

```

new file mode 100644
index 0000000..d2d2cc0
--- /dev/null
+++ b/eval/streaming_sst/eval_auto_glossary_switch.py
@@ -0,0 +1,307 @@
+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+"""Router-only ACL/NLP <-> medicine auto-glossary switch evaluation."""
+
+from __future__ import annotations
+
+import argparse
+import json
+import sys
+from dataclasses import dataclass
+from pathlib import Path
+from typing import Any, Dict, Iterable, List, Optional, Sequence
+
+PROJECT_ROOT = Path(__file__).resolve().parents[2]
+if str(PROJECT_ROOT) not in sys.path:
+    sys.path.insert(0, str(PROJECT_ROOT))
+
+from framework.agents.term_memory.topic_router import (
+    DomainProbeScore,
+    DomainSlice,
+    HybridWindowTopicRouter,
+    RouterConfig,
+    RouterSessionState,
+)
+
+
+ACL_FIXTURE = (
+    "We evaluate BERT and transformer language models on a corpus benchmark for machine translation.",
+    "The parser uses dependency parsing, entity recognition, token embeddings, and BLEU evaluation.",
+    "Pretraining and fine tuning improve encoder decoder attention on the annotation dataset.",
+)
+
+MEDICINE_FIXTURE = (
+    "The patient received clinical treatment for diabetes after diagnosis in the hospital.",
+    "The oncology trial studies cancer infection symptoms, blood pressure, and heart rate.",
+    "Doctors prescribe a tablet dose in mg after surgery and vaccine treatment.",
+)
+
+
+@dataclass(frozen=True)
+class TextWindow:
+    expected_domain: str
+    text: str
+
+
+def build_router(*, min_confidence: float = 0.60, with_probe: bool = False) -> HybridWindowTopicRouter:
+    weight_overrides = {}
+    if with_probe:
+        weight_overrides = {
+            "domain_probe_weight": 0.25,
+            "text_topic_weight": 0.60,
+            "speech_centroid_weight": 0.10,
+            "metadata_prior_weight": 0.05,
+        }
+    return HybridWindowTopicRouter(
+        [
+            DomainSlice("nlp_core_10k", "nlp", centroid=[1.0, 0.0], index_path="mock://nlp"),
+            DomainSlice("medicine_core_10k", "medicine", centroid=[0.0, 1.0], index_path="mock://medicine"),
+        ],
+        RouterConfig(
+            warmup_sec=0.0,
+            update_interval_sec=0.0,
+            switch_cooldown_sec=0.0,
+            min_confidence=min_confidence,
+            min_margin=0.15,
+            min_current_margin=0.10,
+            min_consistent_windows_with_text=2,
+            min_consistent_windows_audio_only=3,
+            **weight_overrides,
+        ),
+    )
+
+
+def read_windows(path: str, domain: str, *, max_windows: int, fallback: Sequence[str]) -> List[TextWindow]:
+    source = Path(path) if path else None
+    lines: List[str] = []
+    if source:
+        if not source.is_file():
+            raise FileNotFoundError(f"text window file not found: {source}")
+        lines = [line.strip() for line in source.read_text(encoding="utf-8").splitlines() if line.strip()]
+    if not lines:
+        lines = list(fallback)
+    return [TextWindow(domain, text) for text in lines[:max(1, int(max_windows))]]
+
+
+def scenario_windows(
+    scenario: str,
+    *,
+    acl_windows: Sequence[TextWindow],
+    medicine_windows: Sequence[TextWindow],
+) -> List[TextWindow]:
+    if scenario == "acl_only":
+        return list(acl_windows)
+    if scenario == "medicine_only":
+        return list(medicine_windows)
+    if scenario == "acl_to_medicine":
+        return list(acl_windows) + list(medicine_windows)
+    if scenario == "medicine_to_acl":
+        return list(medicine_windows) + list(acl_windows)
+    raise ValueError(f"unknown scenario: {scenario}")
+
+
+def initial_state_for(scenario: str) -> RouterSessionState:
+    if scenario.startswith("medicine"):
+        return RouterSessionState("medicine_core_10k", "medicine", created_s=0.0)
+    return RouterSessionState("nlp_core_10k", "nlp", created_s=0.0)
+
+
+def probe_for(window: TextWindow) -> Dict[str, DomainProbeScore]:
+    domain = window.expected_domain
+    preset = f"{domain}_core_10k"
+    return {
+        domain: DomainProbeScore(
+            domain=domain,
+            preset_id=preset,
+            top_score=0.9,
+            mean_topk_score=0.8,
+            top_terms=(f"{domain} probe term",),
+        )
+    }
+
+
+def apply_switch(state: RouterSessionState, target_preset: str, target_domain: str, now_s: float) -> None:
+    state.active_preset_id = target_preset
+    state.active_domain_id = target_domain
+    state.last_switch_s = now_s
+    state.pending_preset_id = None
+
+
+def evaluate_scenario(
+    scenario: str,
+    windows: Sequence[TextWindow],
+    *,
+    router_text_source: str = "manifest_source",
+    with_probe: bool = False,
+    max_switch_windows: int = 2,
+) -> Dict[str, Any]:
+    router = build_router(with_probe=with_probe)
+    state = initial_state_for(scenario)
+    initial_domain = state.active_domain_id
+    records: List[Dict[str, Any]] = []
+    switch_count = 0
+    first_boundary: Optional[int] = None
+    first_target_active: Optional[int] = None
+
+    for idx, window in enumerate(windows, start=1):
+        if first_boundary is None and window.expected_domain != initial_domain:
+            first_boundary = idx
+        decision = router.observe(
+            state,
+            None,
+            [],
+            now_s=float(idx),
+            router_text=window.text,
+            router_text_source=router_text_source,
+            domain_probe_scores=probe_for(window) if with_probe else {},
+        )
+        if decision.action == "switch":
+            switch_count += 1
+            apply_switch(state, decision.target_preset_id, decision.target_domain_id, float(idx))
+        active_domain = state.active_domain_id
+        if first_boundary is not None and first_target_active is None and active_domain == window.expected_domain:
+            first_target_active = idx
+        records.append(
+            {
+                "window": idx,
+                "expected_domain": window.expected_domain,
+                "active_domain": active_domain,
+                "decision_action": decision.action,
+                "decision_target_domain": decision.target_domain_id,
+                "confidence": decision.confidence,
+                "margin": decision.margin,
+                "reason": decision.reason,
+                "text": window.text,
+            }
+        )
+
+    accuracy = (
+        sum(1 for item in records if item["active_domain"] == item["expected_domain"]) / len(records)
+        if records
+        else 0.0
+    )
+    acl_records = [item for item in records if item["expected_domain"] == "nlp"]
+    medicine_records = [item for item in records if item["expected_domain"] == "medicine"]
+    false_medicine_on_acl = sum(1 for item in acl_records if item["active_domain"] == "medicine")
+    false_nlp_on_medicine = sum(1 for item in medicine_records if item["active_domain"] == "nlp")
+    pre_boundary = [
+        item for item in records
+        if first_boundary is None or int(item["window"]) < first_boundary
+    ]
+    false_medicine_on_acl_pre_boundary = sum(
+        1 for item in pre_boundary
+        if item["expected_domain"] == "nlp" and item["active_domain"] == "medicine"
+    )
+    false_nlp_on_medicine_pre_boundary = sum(
+        1 for item in pre_boundary
+        if item["expected_domain"] == "medicine" and item["active_domain"] == "nlp"
+    )
+    switch_latency_windows = None
+    if first_boundary is not None and first_target_active is not None:
+        switch_latency_windows = first_target_active - first_boundary + 1
+    target_domain = windows[-1].expected_domain if windows else initial_domain
+    switch_success = bool(first_boundary is None or state.active_domain_id == target_domain)
+    regression_pass = bool(
+        false_medicine_on_acl_pre_boundary == 0
+        and false_nlp_on_medicine_pre_boundary == 0
+        and switch_success
+        and (switch_latency_windows is None or switch_latency_windows <= max_switch_windows)
+    )
+    return {
+        "scenario": scenario,
+        "router_text_source": router_text_source,
+        "with_probe": with_probe,
+        "windows": len(records),
+        "domain_accuracy": round(accuracy, 4),
+        "switch_count": switch_count,
+        "switch_success": switch_success,
+        "switch_latency_windows": switch_latency_windows,
+        "max_switch_windows": max_switch_windows,
+        "false_medicine_on_acl": false_medicine_on_acl,
+        "false_nlp_on_medicine": false_nlp_on_medicine,
+        "false_medicine_on_acl_pre_boundary": false_medicine_on_acl_pre_boundary,
+        "false_nlp_on_medicine_pre_boundary": false_nlp_on_medicine_pre_boundary,
+        "regression_pass": regression_pass,
+        "records": records,
+    }
+
+
+def run_all_scenarios(
+    *,
+    acl_windows: Sequence[TextWindow],
+    medicine_windows: Sequence[TextWindow],
+    scenarios: Iterable[str],
+    router_text_source: str = "manifest_source",
+    with_probe: boo

...[truncated .codex/reviews/review-packet-20260706-200817.md to 30000 chars]...

## Context: AGENTS.md

```text
# RASST-Demo Agent Instructions

This repository is the demo-system continuation of the previous InfiniSST
EMNLP System Demonstration draft. The current working name is `rasst-demo`.
Treat it as a live demo project for retrieval-aware, terminology-sensitive
streaming speech translation, not as a generic InfiniSST archive.

## Communication

- Prefer English for user-facing explanations unless Chinese is clearly faster,
  more precise, or requested.
- If the user's English or mixed English/Chinese wording is unnatural,
  ambiguous, or unprofessional, include a concise `Better English:` correction.
- Keep language feedback separate from engineering work.
- If an instruction is ambiguous enough to affect paths, code, experiments, or
  paper claims, ask a targeted clarification question before acting.

## Canonical Paths

- Repo root: `/mnt/taurus/home/jiaxuanluo/rasst-demo`
- Demo paper draft: `/mnt/taurus/home/jiaxuanluo/rasst-demo/demo_paper_emnlp`
- Main RASST reference: `/mnt/data2/jiaxuanluo/RASST`
- User-expected RASST home path, if later symlinked or moved:
  `/mnt/taurus/home/jiaxuanluo/RASST`
- Optional RL/post-training reference: `/mnt/taurus/home/jiaxuanluo/RAPO`

Use host-qualified Taurus paths in scripts, docs, and reports. Do not write new
commands using bare `/home/...` or Aries-only `/mnt/aries/...` paths unless the
task explicitly concerns Aries storage.

Large generated files, model checkpoints, logs, recordings, and benchmark dumps
should stay out of the repo unless the user explicitly asks to commit or package
them. Prefer a separate runtime/data root under `/mnt/taurus/data2/jiaxuanluo`
for new large artifacts.

## Current Demo Scope

The baseline system is an InfiniSST-style multi-user simultaneous speech
translation demo with:

- web and Electron frontends;
- microphone, file, YouTube/web, and desktop system-audio input paths;
- a scheduler/back-end split for concurrent sessions;
- prefill/decode batching, KV-cache reuse, attention-sink/sliding-window
  inference, and paged attention support;
- prior 32-sessions-per-GPU positioning from the old draft.

For a new demo-track submission, do not rely on "long speech translation with an
LLM" or "32 sessions per GPU" as the main novelty. Treat those as baseline
system strengths. The refreshed claim should focus on term-dense vertical-domain
translation: domain glossary retrieval, live terminology control, term-recall
diagnostics, and a demo experience that makes terminology corrections visible.

## Extension Direction

Prioritize a practical RASST-Demo story:

```text
streaming speech -> candidate terms/retrieved evidence -> terminology-aware
translation -> live UI diagnostics for latency, term recall, and corrections
```

Good demo features include:

- domain or glossary selection for medical, legal, academic, or financial
  speech;
- live display of retrieved terms/evidence next to the translation;
- user-visible term correction or acceptance controls;
- per-session diagnostics for latency, throughput, term recall, and false-copy
  behavior;
- comparison between plain InfiniSST and terminology-aware/RAG modes.

Avoid making RL the core demo requirement unless experiments already show a
clear user-facing win. RAPO-style RL/post-training is optional and should be
framed as a low-latency 4B student or adaptive policy extension. A 30B model can
remain the stronger teacher, reference model, or quality baseline when that is
more compelling for a demo.

## Relationship To RAPO

RAPO is a post-training reference, not the main identity of this demo repo. If
used, frame RAPO-style work as optional retrieval-aware or terminology-aware
post-training for a smaller student model.

The Speech LLM is the agent. Terminology retrieval, glossary lookup, or domain
evidence is a tool/evidence source. DPO, SimPO, GRPO, and OPD are training
backends; they are not the demo contribution by themselves.

For a compute-conscious extension, prefer:

```text
30B RASST/Qwen-Omni system as demo engine or teacher
4B student as low-latency optional variant
offline teacher/rubric feedback for term recall, false-copy behavior, latency,
and correction quality
```

Do not plan full 30B online GRPO unless the user explicitly changes the scope.

## Paper Framing

The paper in `demo_paper_emnlp` is a starting point, not a final submission.
When revising it:

- update the title away from pure high-throughput InfiniSST scheduling if the
  demo is now RASST/terminology centered;
- keep the 32-session scheduling result as a systems capability, not the whole
  contribution;
- add concrete evaluation, because EMNLP demo submissions can be desk rejected
  if they report no evaluation;
- include screenshots or diagrams of the actual updated demo;
- include a live demo link or installable package plan;
- keep the submission within the current demo-track page limit and style rules;
- state licensing and deployment constraints clearly.

The likely contribution shape is:

1. an interactive streaming speech translation demo for term-dense domains;
2. retrieval-aware terminology assistance integrated into a low-latency SST UI;
3. system evidence showing the quality-latency-terminology trade-off under
   concurrent use.

## Engineering Rules

- Read the existing code before editing; this repo contains a web server,
  Electron app, model wrappers, scheduler, and paper draft.
- Keep changes scoped to the demo path unless the user explicitly asks to sync
  with another repo.
- Prefer small smoke tests before reporting success.
- After committing material code, config, docs, evaluation summaries, or
  progress records, push the branch to the GitHub remote before reporting the
  task complete unless the user explicitly says not to push. Local-only commits
  are not a source of truth for this project.
- Do not commit generated logs, caches, model weights, downloaded checkpoints,
  large media, or temporary LaTeX build products.
- If borrowing code from InfiniSST, RASST, or RAPO, record the source path and
  keep the demo-facing behavior clear.

## Useful Entry Points

- Backend API: `serve/api.py`
- Inference engine: `serve/inference_engine.py`
- Scheduler: `serve/scheduler.py`
- Main agents: `agents/infinisst.py`, `agents/infinisst_fast.py`,
  `agents/infinisst_faster.py`
- Web/static frontend: `serve/static/`
- Electron frontend: `electron/`
- Old demo paper: `demo_paper_emnlp/latex/`
- Integration tests: `test_integrated_system.py`, `test_scheduler_system.py`

When evaluating submission readiness, inspect both the runnable demo and the
paper draft. The submission should be judged by what a reviewer can see in the
live demo/video, not only by model-training claims.

```
